# Text Elements
12, 22, 3, 45, 67, 2 ^qk8YaVAC

Time Complexity: O(n^2) ^QNadt0y2

Bubble Sort ^RXCDVf9m

Difficulty: Very Low ^Cgb6hSJn

Implementation Steps ^xtFRHIgq

Loop through the array, and swap
the current value and the next
value, if the current value is 
larger than next. 

By the end of the array, the single
largest number will be at the end 
of the array. This means we can do
the sort again, but truncated by 1.

Continue doing the swapping of values
each time, reducing the length your are
sorting by each time by 1. Once the 
current length is 1, you can stop. ^5QZ7MsVH

Solution In Code ^fEnmOIwn

Is 12 bigger than 22?
No. Continue ^O1cCmiCc

12, 22, 3, 45, 67, 2 ^zV9p6j5Z

Is 22 bigger than 3?
Yes! Swap the positions and continue. ^c1TWs0pb

12, 3, 22, 45, 67, 2 ^vcAaonjt

Is 22 bigger than 45?
No. Continue. ^XHKCFwox

12, 3, 22, 45, 67, 2 ^6i3mlC8P

Is 45 bigger than 67?
No. Continue. ^650LMXHY

12, 3, 22, 45, 67, 2 ^n1LVycwu

Is 67 bigger than 2?
Yes. Swap positions and continue. ^7UNQmAGt

12, 3, 22, 45, 2, 67 ^vOFWPuRG

New Array To Swap Numbers In ^97dPwdBd

Step 1 ^chdTrOYK

Step 2 ^ZnKCPRzY

Step 3 ^sbNc2Rz0
